var slide_ad = function(available){
  if(available!=1) return true;
  if(YYETS.Util.getCookie('yyets_slide_ad')==1) return true;
  var image = 'http://copy.ousns.com/new/xiala-20141009.jpg';
  var url = 'http://52meiju.taobao.com/'
  var timeout = 8;//秒
  var expire = 2;//小时
  var slide_html = '<div id="yyets_slide_ad" style="width:980px;margin:10px auto;text-align:center;"><p><a href="'+url+'" target="_blank"><img src="'+image+'"></a></p><p style="float:right;width:70px;height:30px;cursor:pointer;font-size:14px;font-weight:bold;border:2px solid #EBEBEB;line-height:30px;">关&nbsp;闭</p></div>';
  $('.topBox').before(slide_html);
  $('#yyets_slide_ad p:last').click(function(){
    $('#yyets_slide_ad').remove();
    YYETS.Util.setCookie('yyets_slide_ad',1,1000*60*60*expire);
  });
  setTimeout(function(){
    $('#yyets_slide_ad').animate({height:'0px'},'slow',function(){
      YYETS.Util.setCookie('yyets_slide_ad',1,1000*60*60*expire);
      $(this).remove()
    });
  },timeout*1000);
}
$(document).ready(function(){slide_ad(1);})//1-开启,0-关闭

<script>
window.openWind=function(url){
	var top=(document.body.clientHeight-420)/2;
	var left=(document.body.clientWidth-520)/2;
	window.open(url,'connect_window', 'height=420, width=560, toolbar =no, menubar=no, scrollbars=yes, resizable=no,top='+top+',left='+left+', location=no, status=no');
	setTimeout(function(){
		$('#shadow').remove();
		}, 300);
};
window.sinaLogin=function(){
	openWind(YYETS.CONST.WWW_URL+"user/connect/weibo?back="+window.location);
};
window.qqLogin=function(){
	openWind(YYETS.CONST.WWW_URL+"user/connect/qq?back="+window.location);
};

$('#logType a').click(function(){
  if($(this).attr('type')=='weibo')
  {
    sinaLogin();
	return;
  }
  if($(this).attr('type')=='qq')
  {
    qqLogin();
	return;
  }
  $(this).parent().hide();
  $('#logType dt').text($(this).text()).attr('type',$(this).attr('type'));
  $('input[type=hidden][name=type]').val($(this).attr('type'));
});

$('#loginArea input[name=login]').click(function(){
  YYETS.Loading();
  type = $('#loginArea input[name=type]').val();
  account = $('#loginArea input[name=account]').val();
  password = $('#loginArea input[name=password]').val();
  remember = $('#loginArea input[name=remember]').attr('checked')=='checked'?1:0;
  $.post(YYETS.CONST.WWW_URL+'user/login/ajaxLogin',{type:type,account:account,password:password,type:type,remember:remember},function(data){
    if(data.status==1){
      window.history.go(0);
    }else{
      YYETS.ShowMsg(data.info);
      YYETS.Loading('hide');
    }
  },'json');
  return false;
});

$('#logout').click(function(){
  YYETS.Loading();
  $.getJSON(YYETS.CONST.WWW_URL+'user/logout/ajaxLogout',function(data){
    if(data.status==1){
      window.history.go(0);
    }
    YYETS.Loading('hide');
  });
  return false;
});


$.ajax({
	url: YYETS.CONST.WWW_URL+'user/login/getCurUserTopInfo',
	async: false, 
	dataType: "json",
	success: function(data){
		if(data.status==1){
			$('#top_nickname').text(data.data.userinfo.nickname);
			$('#top_userpic').attr('src',data.data.userinfo.avatar_t);
			$('#navbar_msg').text(data.data.message_unread_num);
      if(data.data.message_unread_num>0) $('#navbar_msg').parent().addClass('f1');
			$('#navbar_fol').text(data.data.follow_unread_num);
      if(data.data.follow_unread_num>0) $('#navbar_fol').parent().addClass('f1');
			$('#navbar_rt').text(data.data.reply_unread_num);
      if(data.data.reply_unread_num>0) $('#navbar_rt').parent().addClass('f1');
			$('.topNav:eq(1)').show();
      if(data.data.post!='') $('#post_List').html(data.data.post);
      if(data.data.login_score>0) YYETS.JQUERY.SCORETIPS('每日登录',data.data.login_score,1500);
			YYETS.CONST.USER = data.data.userinfo;
		}else{
			$('.topNav:eq(0)').show();
		}
    YYETS.JQUERY.RANDOMSHOW($('.topNav:visible .top_log_news a'));
	}
});

    if(_type!='') $(this).find('dd a[type='+_type+']').addClass('cur').siblings().removeClass('cur');
    $(this).find('dt').addClass('HT').next().show();
  },out:function(){
    $(this).find('dt').removeClass('HT').next().hide();
  },delay_time:200});
});

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
  var matches = window.location.href.match(/http:\/\/[^/]+(\/.*)/);
  var group_name = matches==null?'':matches[1].replace(/\/{2,}/m,'/');
  var groups = {'news':'/news','subtitle':'/subtitle','movielist':'/movie/list','help':'/help','bbs':'/bbs','today':'/today','work':'/work','resourcelist':'/resource','schedule':'/schedule|/html/return|/html/new','fav':'/user/fav','Announcement':'/Announcement'};
  for(key in groups)
  {
    regx = new RegExp(groups[key],'i');
    if(group_name.search(regx)!=-1)
    {
      $('.menuBox li[channel='+key+'] a').addClass('cur');
      return;
    }
  }
  $('.menuBox li:first a').addClass('cur');
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function(){
	if((typeof channel!=undefined) && (channel=='movie'||channel=='openclass'||channel=='tv')) $('#yyets_share').prepend('<a style="background:url('+YYETS.CONST.RES_URL+'images/rss.png) no-repeat;" href="'+YYETS.CONST.WWW_URL+'rss/'+rid+'" rel="rss" target="_blank"></a>');
	$('#yyets_share a[rel!=rss]').click(function(){
		var url = '';
		var title = encodeURIComponent(share.title+' 分享地址:'+share.url+(channel=='tv'||channel=='movie'?' #'+share.cnname+'#':'')+',#YYeTs# #人人影视# '+YYETS.CONST.WWW_URL);
    if(channel=='movie'||channel=='openclass'||channel=='tv') title += ' 其他网站下载: http://www.yayaxz.com/resource/'+rid;
		switch($(this).attr('rel')){
			case 'weibo':
				url = 'http://service.weibo.com/share/share.php?title='+title+'&pic='+share.pic;
				break;
			case 'tqq':
				url = 'http://share.v.t.qq.com/index.php?c=share&a=index&title='+title+'&url=&appkey=a75e1c5904c842b7b3aed10213379cca&site='+YYETS.CONST.WWW_URL+'&pic='+share.pic;
				break;
			case 'renren':
				url = 'http://share.renren.com/share/buttonshare.do?link='+share.url+'&title='+title;
				break;
		}
		if(url!='') share_window(url);
	});
});
var share_window=function(share_url){
	window.open(share_url,'_blank','scrollbars=no,width=600,height=450,left=75,top=20,status=no,resizable=yes');
}
</script>
